scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*} \mathcal{L}_{\boldsymbol{u}} g_{\mu \nu} &amp;= \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}} u^{\sigma} + \frac{\partial u^{\alpha}}{\partial x^{\mu}} g_{\alpha \nu} + \frac{\partial u^{\beta}}{\partial x^{\nu}} g_{\mu \beta} \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}} u^{\sigma} + \frac{\partial u^{\alpha}}{\partial x^{\mu}} g_{\alpha \nu} + u^{\alpha} \frac{\partial g_{\alpha \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} - u^{\alpha} \frac{\partial g_{\alpha \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial u^{\beta}}{\partial x^{\nu}} g_{\mu \beta} + u^{\beta} \frac{\partial g_{\mu \beta}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - u^{\beta} \frac{\partial g_{\mu \beta}}{\partial x^{\nu}} \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}} u^{\sigma} + \frac{\partial}{\partial x^{\mu}} (u^{\alpha} g_{\alpha \nu}) - u^{\alpha} \frac{\partial g_{\alpha \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial}{\partial x^{\nu}} (u^{\beta} g_{\mu \beta}) - u^{\beta} \frac{\partial g_{\mu \beta}}{\partial x^{\nu}} \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}} u^{\sigma} + \frac{\partial u_{\nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} - u^{\alpha} \frac{\partial g_{\alpha \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial u_{\mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - u^{\beta} \frac{\partial g_{\mu \beta}}{\partial x^{\nu}} \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial u_{\nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial u_{\mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} + u^{\sigma} \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}} - u^{\sigma} \frac{\partial g_{\sigma \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} - u^{\sigma} \frac{\partial g_{\mu \sigma}}{\partial x^{\nu}} \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial u_{\nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial u_{\mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - u^{\sigma} \left(\frac{\partial g_{\sigma \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial g_{\mu \sigma}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}}\right) \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial u_{\nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial u_{\mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - 2 u_{\lambda} \frac{1}{2} g^{\sigma \lambda} \left(\frac{\partial g_{\sigma \mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} + \frac{\partial g_{\sigma \nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} - \frac{\partial g_{\mu \nu}}{\partial x^{\sigma}}\right) \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial u_{\nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} + \frac{\partial u_{\mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - 2 u_{\lambda} \Gamma^{\lambda}{}_{\mu \nu} \\ &amp;= \frac{\partial u_{\nu}}{\partial x^{\mu}} - u_{\lambda} \Gamma^{\lambda}{}_{\mu \nu} + \frac{\partial u_{\mu}}{\partial x^{\nu}} - u_{\lambda} \Gamma^{\lambda}{}_{\nu \mu} \\ &amp;= \nabla_{\mu} u_{\nu} + \nabla_{\nu} u_{\mu} \\ &amp;= 0, \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:25.2115em;vertical-align:-12.3557em;"></span><span
